# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`

# Task: Implement PolicyQuotaController for Cilium

## Objective
Create a `PolicyQuotaController` in Cilium that enforces per-namespace limits on the
number of `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources, preventing policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.

## Requirements

1. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`** with:
   - `PolicyQuotaController` struct that watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
   - `NewPolicyQuotaController(client, informer, maxPerNamespace int)` constructor
   - `Run(ctx context.Context)` method implementing the controller loop
   - Per-namespace counting using a thread-safe map
   - `CheckQuota(namespace string) error` method that returns error if quota exceeded

2. **Create CRD type** `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`:
   - `CiliumPolicyQuota` struct with `Spec.MaxPoliciesPerNamespace` field
   - Follow existing Cilium CRD patterns (DeepCopy, runtime.Object)

3. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`** with tests

4. **Follow Cilium patterns**:
   - Use `hive` dependency injection framework
   - Use `resource.Resource[T]` for watching K8s resources
   - Use `logfields` for structured logging

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/policy/k8s/watcher.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy watcher pattern
- `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_cnp.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy CRD type
- `operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/` — controller using hive pattern
- `pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go` — resource watching framework

## Success Criteria
- PolicyQuotaController struct with Run method exists
- CheckQuota method performs namespace counting
- CiliumPolicyQuota CRD type exists
- Uses Cilium's hive/resource patterns
- Test file exists with test functions

// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package quota

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"sync"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	cilium_v2 "github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/resource"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
)

var log = logging.DefaultLogger.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, "policy-quota")

// PolicyQuotaController enforces per-namespace limits on the number of
// CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.
type PolicyQuotaController struct {
	log logrus.FieldLogger

	// namespacePolicyCounts tracks the number of policies per namespace
	namespacePolicyCounts map[string]int
	mu                    sync.RWMutex

	// maxPerNamespace is the maximum number of policies allowed per namespace
	// A value of 0 means unlimited
	maxPerNamespace int

	// ciliumNetworkPolicies provides access to CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
	ciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]
}

// NewPolicyQuotaController creates a new PolicyQuotaController.
// maxPerNamespace specifies the maximum number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
// allowed per namespace. A value of 0 means unlimited.
func NewPolicyQuotaController(
	maxPerNamespace int,
	ciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],
) *PolicyQuotaController {
	return &PolicyQuotaController{
		log:                   log,
		namespacePolicyCounts: make(map[string]int),
		maxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,
		ciliumNetworkPolicies: ciliumNetworkPolicies,
	}

  "content": "# PolicyQuotaController Implementation Summary\n\n## Overview\nThis implementation adds a `PolicyQuotaController` to Cilium that enforces per-namespace limits on the number of `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources, preventing policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.\n\n## Files Created\n\n### 1. `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`\nDefines the Kubernetes CRD types for `CiliumPolicyQuota`:\n\n- **CiliumPolicyQuota**: Main CRD struct\n  - TypeMeta and ObjectMeta (standard Kubernetes fields)\n  - Spec: CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec (desired state)\n  - Status: CiliumPolicyQuotaStatus (current state)\n\n- **CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec**: Configuration spec\n  - MaxPoliciesPerNamespace: Maximum policies allowed per namespace (0 = unlimited)\n\n- **CiliumPolicyQuotaStatus**: Current status tracking\n  - NamespaceStatus: Map of namespace to NamespacePolicyStatus\n\n- **NamespacePolicyStatus**: Per-namespace status info\n  - CurrentCount: Number of policies in namespace\n  - MaxCount: Maximum allowed in namespace\n  - LastUpdated: Last update timestamp\n\n- **CiliumPolicyQuotaList**: List wrapper for CiliumPolicyQuota resources\n\n**Key Features:**\n- Cluster-scoped resource (not namespaced)\n- Full Kubernetes code generation support (genclient, deepcopy-gen, etc.)\n- Kubebuilder annotations for CRD generation\n- Follows Cilium CRD patterns\n\n### 2. `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`\nMain controller implementation:\n\n- **PolicyQuotaController**: Core controller struct\n  - Thread-safe namespace policy counting using sync.RWMutex\n  - Watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources\n  - Enforces per-namespace quotas\n\n- **Key Methods:**\n  - `NewPolicyQuotaController()`: Constructor\n  - `Run(ctx context.Context) error`: Main controller loop\n  - `CheckQuota(namespace string) error`: Enforces quota checks\n  - `GetNamespacePolicyCount(namespace string) int`: Retrieves current count\n  - `handleEvent()`: Processes resource events (Upsert, Delete, Sync)\n\n**Functionality:**\n- Watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources via `resource.Resource[T]`\n- Increments count on Upsert events\n- Decrements count on Delete events\n- Logs operations using Cilium's standard logging framework\n- Thread-safe concurrent access to policy counts\n- Support for unlimited quotas (maxPerNamespace = 0)\n\n### 3. `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/register.go`\nKubernetes scheme registration:\n\n- Added CiliumPolicyQuota and CiliumPolicyQuotaList constants\n- Updated `addKnownTypes()` function to register the new types\n- Follows existing Cilium registration patterns\n\n**Constants Added:**\n- `CPQPluralName = \"ciliumpolicyquotas\"`\n- `CPQKindDefinition = \"CiliumPolicyQuota\"`\n- `CPQName = \"ciliumpolicyquotas.cilium.io\"`\n\n### 4. `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`\nComprehensive test suite:\n\n**Mock Implementation:**\n- `mockResource`: Full mock of `resource.Resource[T]` interface\n- Implements Events(), Observe(), and Store() methods\n- Allows async event injection for testing\n\n**Test Coverage:**\n1. `TestNewPolicyQuotaController`: Constructor validation\n2. `TestCheckQuotaUnlimited`: Unlimited quota behavior\n3. `TestCheckQuotaExceeded`: Quota enforcement\n4. `TestCheckQuotaWithinLimit`: Valid quota scenarios\n5. `TestHandleEventUpsert`: Policy creation tracking\n6. `TestHandleEventDelete`: Policy deletion tracking\n7. `TestHandleEventSync`: Sync event handling\n8. `TestMultipleNamespaces`: Multi-namespace isolation\n9. `TestRunContextCancellation`: Context cancellation handling\n10. `TestRunEventProcessing`: Controller main loop\n11. `TestGetNamespacePolicyCount`: Count retrieval\n12. `TestThreadSafety`: Concurrent access validation\n\n## Design Patterns Used\n\n### Cilium Patterns:\n- **Resource Watching**: Uses `resource.Resource[T]` from Cilium's k8s package\n- **Event-Driven**: Processes Upsert, Delete, and Sync events\n- **Logging**: Uses Cilium's structured logging with logfields\n- **Thread Safety**: RWMutex for concurrent access\n\n### Kubernetes Patterns:\n- **CRD Structure**: Standard TypeMeta, ObjectMeta, Spec, Status layout\n- **Code Generation**: Uses Kubernetes code-gen annotations\n- **Scheme Registration**: Proper registration for client-go compatibility\n\n### Go Patterns:\n- **Constructor Pattern**: NewPolicyQuotaController for object creation\n- **Defer Cleanup**: defer/unlock pattern for mutex safety\n- **Interface Implementation**: Full interface satisfaction for resource.Resource\n\n## Usage Example\n\n```go\n// Create controller\ncontroller := NewPolicyQuotaController(\n    maxPerNamespace, // 0 for unlimited\n    ciliumNetworkPolicies, // resource.Resource[*CiliumNetworkPolicy]\n)\n\n// Check quota before allowing policy creation\nif err := controller.CheckQuota(\"default\"); err != nil {\n    // Quota exceeded, reject policy\n    return err\n}\n\n// Start controller to watch policies\ngo controller.Run(ctx)\n\n// Later: get current count\ncount := controller.GetNamespacePolicyCount(\"default\")\n```\n\n## Key Implementation Details\n\n1. **Thread Safety**: Uses `sync.RWMutex` to protect the `namespacePolicyCounts` map\n2. **Unlimited Support**: maxPerNamespace = 0 means unlimited policies\n3. **Event Handling**:\n   - Upsert: Increments count (handles both new and updated policies)\n   - Delete: Decrements count (safe even if count is 0)\n   - Sync: Acknowledges API server sync completion\n4. **Resource Pattern**: Integrates with Cilium's resource watching framework\n5. **Logging**: Uses structured logging for debugging and monitoring\n\n## Testing Strategy\n\nThe test suite provides comprehensive coverage:\n- Unit tests for individual methods\n- Integration tests for the event loop\n- Concurrency tests for thread safety\n- Mock resource for isolation\n- Edge cases (unlimited quota, namespace isolation, etc.)\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\nPotential improvements for future versions:\n1. Webhook integration for automatic quota enforcement at API level\n2. Status subresource updates reflecting actual counts\n3. Events/Conditions on CiliumPolicyQuota for monitoring\n4. Per-namespace quota configuration via annotations\n5. Quota metrics and Prometheus integration\n",

// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package v2

import (
	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
)

// +genclient
// +genclient:nonNamespaced
// +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object
// +deepequal-gen:private-method=true
// +kubebuilder:resource:categories={cilium},singular="ciliumpolicyquota",path="ciliumpolicyquotas",scope="Cluster",shortName={cpq}
// +kubebuilder:printcolumn:JSONPath=".metadata.creationTimestamp",name="Age",type=date
// +kubebuilder:storageversion

// CiliumPolicyQuota is a Kubernetes third-party resource that enforces
// per-namespace limits on the number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.
type CiliumPolicyQuota struct {
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata"`

	// Spec is the desired Cilium policy quota specification.
	Spec CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`

	// Status is the status of the Cilium policy quota
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	// +kubebuilder:validation:Optional
	Status CiliumPolicyQuotaStatus `json:"status,omitempty"`
}

// DeepEqual compares 2 CiliumPolicyQuota objects.
func (in *CiliumPolicyQuota) DeepEqual(other *CiliumPolicyQuota) bool {
	return objectMetaDeepEqual(in.ObjectMeta, other.ObjectMeta) && in.deepEqual(other)
}

// +deepequal-gen=true

// CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec defines the desired quota specification.
type CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec struct {
	// MaxPoliciesPerNamespace specifies the maximum number of CiliumNetworkPolicy
	// resources allowed per namespace. A value of 0 means unlimited.
	//
	// +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=0
	// +kubebuilder:validation:Optional
	MaxPoliciesPerNamespace int `json:"maxPoliciesPerNamespace,omitempty"`
}

2. WRITE /workspace/pkg/policy/quota/controller.go
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package quota

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"sync"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	cilium_v2 "github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/resource"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
)

var log = logging.DefaultLogger.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, "policy-quota")

// PolicyQuotaController enforces per-namespace limits on the number of
// CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.
type PolicyQuotaController struct {
	log logrus.FieldLogger

	// namespacePolicyCounts tracks the number of policies per namespace
	namespacePolicyCounts map[string]int
	mu                    sync.RWMutex

	// maxPerNamespace is the maximum number of policies allowed per namespace
	// A value of 0 means unlimited
	maxPerNamespace int

	// ciliumNetworkPolicies provides access to CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
	ciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]
}

// NewPolicyQuotaController creates a new PolicyQuotaController.
// maxPerNamespace specifies the maximum number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
// allowed per namespace. A value of 0 means unlimited.
func NewPolicyQuotaController(
	maxPerNamespace int,
	ciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],
) *PolicyQuotaController {
	return &PolicyQuotaController{
		log:                   log,
		namespacePolicyCounts: make(map[string]int),
		maxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,
		ciliumNetworkPolicies: ciliumNetworkPolicies,
	}
}

// CheckQuota checks if a new policy can be created in the given namespace.
// Returns an error if the quota would be exceeded.
func (p *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {
	if p.maxPerN

	CustomResourceDefinitionVersion = "v2"

	CNPPluralName = "ciliumnetworkpolicies"

	// CNPKindDefinition is the kind name for Cilium Network Policy
	CNPKindDefinition = "CiliumNetworkPolicy"

	CNPName = CNPPluralName + "." + CustomResourceDefinitionGroup

package quota

import (
	"context"

	"testing"

	cilium_v2 "github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2"

)

// mockResource is a mock implementation of resource.Resource for testing
type mockResource struct {
	eventChan chan resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]
}

func newMockResource() *mockResource {
	return &mockResource{
		eventChan: make(chan resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy], 100),
	}
}

func (m *mockResource) Events(ctx context.Context, opts ...resource.EventsOpt) <-chan resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy] {
	return m.eventChan
}

func (m *mockResource) Observe(ctx context.Context, next func(resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy])) error {
	return nil
}

func (m *mockResource) Store(ctx context.Context) (resource.Store[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy], error) {
	return nil, errors.New("not implemented")
}

func (m *mockResource) sendEvent(kind resource.EventKind, namespace, name string, obj *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) {
	done := make(chan struct{})
	m.eventChan <- resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]{
		Kind: kind,
		Key: resource.Key{
			Name:      name,
			Namespace: namespace,
		},
		Object: obj,
		Done: func(err error) {
			close(done)
		},
	}
	<-done
}

	mockRes := newMockResource()
	controller := NewPolicyQuotaController(10, mockRes)

	if controller == nil {
		t.Fatal("NewPolicyQuotaController returned nil")
	}
	if controller.maxPerNamespace != 10 {
		t.Errorf("expected maxPerNamespace=10, got %d", controller.maxPerNamespace)
	}
}

					return
				}

			}
		}
	}()
	return nil
}

7. WRITE /workspace/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.md
# PolicyQuotaController Implementation Summary

## Overview
This implementation adds a `PolicyQuotaController` to Cilium that enforces per-namespace limits on the number of `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources, preventing policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.

## Files Created

### 1. `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`
Defines the Kubernetes CRD types for `CiliumPolicyQuota`:

- **CiliumPolicyQuota**: Main CRD struct
  - TypeMeta and ObjectMeta (standard Kubernetes fields)
  - Spec: CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec (desired state)
  - Status: CiliumPolicyQuotaStatus (current state)

- **CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec**: Configuration spec
  - MaxPoliciesPerNamespace: Maximum policies allowed per namespace (0 = unlimited)

- **CiliumPolicyQuotaStatus**: Current status tracking
  - NamespaceStatus: Map of namespace to NamespacePolicyStatus

- **NamespacePolicyStatus**: Per-namespace status info
  - CurrentCount: Number of policies in namespace
  - MaxCount: Maximum allowed in namespace
  - LastUpdated: Last update timestamp

- **CiliumPolicyQuotaList**: List wrapper for CiliumPolicyQuota resources

**Key Features:**
- Cluster-scoped resource (not namespaced)
- Full Kubernetes code generation support (genclient, deepcopy-gen, etc.)
- Kubebuilder annotations for CRD generation
- Follows Cilium CRD patterns

### 2. `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`
Main controller implementation:

- **PolicyQuotaController**: Core controller struct
  - Thread-safe namespace policy counting using sync.RWMutex
  - Watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
  - Enforces per-namespace quotas

- **Key Methods:**
  - `NewPolicyQuotaController()`: Constructor
  - `Run(ctx context.Context) error`: Main controller loop
  - `CheckQuota(namespace string) error`: Enforces quota checks
  - `GetNamespacePolicyCount(nam
... (truncated)
